with registered capital of RMB 50 million %28USD %2410 million approx.%29.  Previously trading as Cangzhou Excellent Plastic Printing Co.%2C Ltd%2C it boasts 22 years of specialised experience in the research%2C development and manufacturing of Flexible Packaging.  Strategically positioned in Dongguang County%2C Hebei Province%2C the largest flexible packaging industrial base in Northern China%2C it assures an abundance of supply chain which effectively guarantee delivery turnaround and cost competitiveness.  Our manufacturing facility is located in Jingnan Technology Industrial Park in Dongguang County%2C adjacent to Beijing-Shanghai Freeway for convenience of logistics.  Covering a site area of 3%2C000%2C000 m2%2C and building area of 20%2C000 m2%2C the workshop is constructed in according with Industrial 4.0 intelligent standards%2C including 8%2C000 m2 of 100%2C000 level dust-free purification workshop.  Equipped with 4 sets of BOBST high-speed printing production lines%2C the printing speed reaches up to 400 m%5C%2Fmin%2C with up to 10 printing colors. There are also dry composite and solvent-free composite equipment available to meet the needs of customers. The workshop is equipped with over 30 sets of high-speed slitting equipments and bag making machines%2C producing a large variety of pouches and bags%2C including flat bottom bag%2C stand up bag%2C zipper bag.  The daily production in formed bag reaches 3 million pcs%2C and the film production capacity reaches 50 tons%5C%2Fday. There are 8 sets of high-definition intelligent digital QC inspection equipments to guarantee no defective products can be missed%2C together with our stringent quality assurance policy ensures ultimate customer satisfaction. %3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3EAdvanced technology allow us to customize various packaging functions such as high barrier%2C anti-leakage%2C anti-static%2C variable QR code%2C high-speed automatic packaging%2C etc.%2C to meet customer%27s various functional requirements for packaging. Our customers are mainly in the food industry%2C there are also some supporting cases in the fields of daily necessities%2C agricultural%2C medical and electronic products.  Our products are sold all over the world and exported to the United States%2C Europe%2C Australia%2C etc. We have established long-term cooperative relationships with well-known brand owners such as Daoxiangcun%2C Zongjiafu%2C Wandashan%2C Jinshahe and Kedi Dairy.%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3EQuality is our life%2C with ISO9001%3A2015 and FSSC22000 certified%2C we also implement the PDCA cycle improvement management system internally.  With the goal of %26quot%3Bgood quality%2C zero defects%26quot%3B to provide consumers with consistent high quality flexible packaging products. %3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3E%3Cbr%3EOur R%26amp%3BD department focuses particularly on the environmental sustainable packaging solutions. The high-barrier recyclable packaging and high-barrier biodegradable packaging has been developed and released in  the domestic market. As a leader in adopting CO catalytic combustion treatment devices to achieve energy saving and emission reduction%2C our business takes a green%2C healthy and sustainable development approach. <script>
    // 买家收藏夹 html espace twice bug fixed
    if(window.location.pathname === '/favorite2/favorite_home.htm' && typeof MutationObserver === 'function') {

        function observeTarget(rootSelector, modifySelector) {
            var $root = document.querySelector(rootSelector)
            var isFirst = true
            var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutationsList) {
                function doReplace() {
                    var nList = document.querySelectorAll(modifySelector)
                    var nListArr = Array.prototype.slice.call(nList, null)
                    nListArr.forEach(function($nodeItem) {
                        $nodeItem.innerHTML = $nodeItem.innerText
                    })
                }
                
                if(isFirst) {
                    setTimeout(doReplace, 2000)
                    isFirst = false
                } else {
                    doReplace()
                }
            })
            
            observer.observe($root, { attributes: true, childList: false, subtree: false })
        }

        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            var rootSelector = '.fav-list-box.product-list-box'
            var modifySelector = '.suppliers-list-box .item-suppliers-name'
            
            observeTarget(rootSelector, modifySelector)
        })

    }
</script>

<script>
    try{
        var loadScript = function (url, callback) {
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = url;
          script.async = true;
          if (script.addEventListener) {
            script.addEventListener('load', function () {
              callback();
            }, false);
          } else if (script.attachEvent) {
            script.attachEvent('onreadystatechange', function () {
              var target = window.event.srcElement;
              if (target.readyState === 'loaded') {
                callback();
              }
            });
          }
          document.body.appendChild(script);
        };
        
        var loadCss = function (url) {
          var style = document.createElement('link');
          style.rel = 'stylesheet';
          style.href = url;
          document.head.appendChild(style);
        }

        window.BzEvaluate = {};
        window.BzEvaluate.loadSurvey = function (params) {
          loadScript('https://air.alibaba.com/app/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/pages_version.html', function () {
            // 加载css
            loadCss('https://s.alicdn.com/@g/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/' + window._BZ_VERSION_.version + '/pages/survey/index.web.css', 'css');
            // 加载js
            loadScript('https://s.alicdn.com/@g/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/'+ window._BZ_VERSION_.version + '/pages/survey/index.web.js', function () {
              // 执行页面渲染
              window.BzEvaluate.render(params);
            });
          });
        }
        
        var bz_survey_config_scene = "";
        
        if(location.href.indexOf('profile.alibaba.com/profile/buyer_selection.htm') > -1){
            // 买家选品
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'ma_buyer_selection_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (/^https:\/\/www.alibaba.com\/trueview\/.*(_\d+.html)$/.test(location.href)) {
            // true view 沉浸页
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'true_view_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (location.href.indexOf('www.alibaba.com/trade/search') > -1) {
            // 搜索页
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'search_list_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (location.hostname == 'www.alibaba.com' && location.pathname === '/') {
            // 首页
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'buyer_pc_home_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (location.href.indexOf('www.alibaba.com/live/') > -1 || location.href.indexOf('watch.alibaba.com/v/') > -1 ) {
            // 直播
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'live_room_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (/^https:\/\/i\.alibaba\.com\/globalBuyerIndex\.htm/.test(location.href)) {
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'buyer_pc_ma_questionnaire_location';
        }
         
        
        if(bz_survey_config_scene){
                                    
            window.BzEvaluate.loadSurvey({
              type: 'dialog',
              link: 'https://air.alibaba.com/app/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/pages_survey.html?bizCode=' + bz_survey_config_scene + '&status=none&targetType=BUYER',
              style: {
                bottom: '100px',
                right: 0,  
              },
              callback: function () {}
            });
        }
    }catch(e){
        
    }
</script>
